      Executed DbCommand (4ms) [Parameters=[@__userId_0='1' (Nullable = true)], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']
      SELECT [c1].[CartId], [c1].[UserId], [s].[CartItemId], [s].[CartId], [s].[ProductId], [s].[Quantity], [s].[ProductId0], [s].[ImageUrl], [s].[Price], [s].[ProductCategoriesId], [s].[ProductDescription], [s].[ProductName], [s].[ProductType]

          FROM [Carts] AS [c]
          WHERE [c].[UserId] = @__userId_0
      ) AS [c1]
      LEFT JOIN (
          SELECT [c0].[CartItemId], [c0].[CartId], [c0].[ProductId], [c0].[Quantity], [p].[ProductId] AS [ProductId0], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[Price], [p].[ProductCategoriesId], [p].[ProductDescription], [p].[ProductName], [p].[ProductType]

          INNER JOIN [Products] AS [p] ON [c0].[ProductId] = [p].[ProductId]
